# 自动国策进度：任务式决议倒计时（结构照抄原版 CHI_improving_inefficient_economy_mission），
# 挂在原版"政治行动"(political_actions)分类下，priority=999 排第一位。决议 id 复用国策 id，
# 标题/描述自动读国策原版本地化，倒计时用任务原生剩余天数显示，不加自定义本地化。
#
# activation/cancel_trigger 同时卡两个条件：
#   - autocore_wip_<id> 旗子：国策完成/条件失效被清理时旗子清掉 -> 任务取消
#   - autocore_focus_paused：玩家手动推进国策时=1 -> 任务取消（原生倒计时没法冻结，只能撤下），
#     恢复自动推进后=0 -> 任务重新激活，days_mission_timeout 读 autocore_focus_remaining
#     （=total-days，01_on_actions.txt 里每日计算），从正确的剩余天数继续倒数而不是满额重来。
# 注意失效清理只在未暂停分支执行（auto_focus_effects 设计如此）：暂停期间条件失效，任务已因
# 暂停被撤下；恢复当天清理先清旗子，任务不会再激活。两条路都兜住。
# 游戏更新后需用最新 target_ids.txt 重新生成本文件。

political_actions = {

	CHI_VTOL_experiments = {
		icon = generic_research
		priority = 999
		allowed = { always = yes }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = autocore_wip_CHI_VTOL_experiments
			check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused < 1 }
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_wip_CHI_VTOL_experiments }
				check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused > 0 }
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = var:autocore_focus_remaining
		timeout_effect = {
		}
	}

		priority = 999
		allowed = { always = yes }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = autocore_wip_FRA_guarantee_the_constitution
			check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused < 1 }
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_wip_FRA_guarantee_the_constitution }
				check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused > 0 }
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = var:autocore_focus_remaining
		timeout_effect = {
		}
	}

		priority = 999
		allowed = { always = yes }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = autocore_wip_JAP_the_ie_system_and_socialism
			check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused < 1 }
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_wip_JAP_the_ie_system_and_socialism }
				check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused > 0 }
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = var:autocore_focus_remaining
		timeout_effect = {
		}
	}

			has_country_flag = autocore_wip_uk_south_africa_focus
			check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused < 1 }
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_wip_uk_south_africa_focus }
				check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused > 0 }
			}
		}
		is_good = yes
		days_mission_timeout = var:autocore_focus_remaining
		timeout_effect = {
		}
	}

	uk_waves_focus = {
		icon = generic_research
		priority = 999
		allowed = { always = yes }
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = autocore_wip_uk_waves_focus

		}
		cancel_trigger = {

				NOT = { has_country_flag = autocore_wip_uk_waves_focus }
				check_variable = { autocore_focus_paused > 0 }

		}

		}
	}
